Speeky-AI Product User Stories & Acceptance Criteria

100 User Stories, Organized by Feature — Complete Specification Document

Onboarding & Account Management



ONB-US-01: User Login & Authentication

STATUS: In Development   PRIORITY: High   ACTOR: Registered User

Intent: To allow a returning user to securely authenticate with their credentials (or SSO) and resume access to their account and learning progress.

Happy Path Steps

Navigation: User opens the app/website and lands on the Login screen.

Credential Entry: User enters their registered email/username and password (or selects "Continue with Apple/Google").

Validation: System validates credentials against the stored (hashed) password or verifies the SSO token.

Session Creation: System creates an authenticated session and issues a secure access/refresh token.

Redirect: User is redirected to their dashboard/home screen with progress and settings restored.

Acceptance Criteria

Passwords must never be transmitted or stored in plain text; validation occurs against a securely hashed value.

A successful login must restore the user's full session context (profile, progress, preferences) without requiring re-setup.

The system must support both email/password login and third-party SSO (Apple/Google) as valid authentication paths.

Access tokens must be short-lived, with refresh tokens used to maintain longer sessions securely.

Exception Handling

E-01: Incorrect Password. User enters a valid email but the wrong password. RESOLUTION: System displays a generic "Incorrect email or password" message (never specifying which field is wrong) and increments a failed-attempt counter.

E-02: Unrecognized Email. User enters an email that is not registered. RESOLUTION: System shows the same generic "Incorrect email or password" message as E-01, avoiding disclosure of which accounts exist.

E-03: Account Locked from Repeated Failures. User exceeds a threshold of failed login attempts (e.g., 5 in 15 minutes). RESOLUTION: Account is temporarily locked, user is notified via on-screen message and email, and offered a password-reset path to regain access.

E-04: Unverified Email Address. User's credentials are correct but their email was never verified after registration. RESOLUTION: Login is blocked and the system prompts the user to verify their email, offering to resend the verification link.

E-05: SSO Provider Failure. The Apple/Google authentication service is unreachable or returns an error. RESOLUTION: System displays "Unable to connect to \[Provider\] right now" and offers email/password login as a fallback.

E-06: Expired or Tampered Session Token. A stored refresh token has expired or fails signature validation. RESOLUTION: System silently invalidates the session and redirects to the Login screen, without exposing internal token details.

E-07: New/Unrecognized Device Login. User logs in successfully from a device or location never seen on this account. RESOLUTION: System sends a security notification email to the account owner and, for high-risk cases, prompts an additional verification step (e.g., one-time code).

E-08: Brute-Force / Bot Traffic Detected. Automated, high-frequency login attempts are detected against one or many accounts. RESOLUTION: System throttles the offending IP/device, injects a CAPTCHA challenge, and alerts the security/monitoring pipeline.

E-09: Network Interruption Mid-Login. User's connection drops after submitting credentials but before a response is received. RESOLUTION: Client retries the request idempotently without creating duplicate sessions, and shows a "Reconnecting…" state rather than a silent failure.

E-10: Password Reset Pending. User attempts to log in with an old password while a password-reset request is still active. RESOLUTION: System accepts the old password until the reset is completed, then invalidates it immediately once the new password is set, logging out other active sessions.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-01

Valid email and password

User is authenticated and redirected to their dashboard.

TC-02

Wrong password entered

Generic error shown; no indication of which field was incorrect.

TC-03

5 failed attempts within 15 minutes

Account is locked and user is offered a password-reset path.

TC-04

Login attempt with unverified email

Login blocked; verification prompt with resend option shown.

TC-05

SSO provider unreachable

Error shown; email/password fallback remains available.

TC-06

Login from a new device

Security notification email sent; step-up verification triggered if high-risk.

TC-07

Automated rapid-fire login attempts

CAPTCHA challenge triggered and offending source throttled.

TC-08

Login with old password during active reset

Old password works once; invalidated immediately after new password is set.



ONB-US-02: Email Verification & Account Activation STATUS: In Development    PRIORITY: High    ACTOR: New Learner

Intent: To confirm the authenticity of a new learner's email address before granting full account access, protecting the platform from fraudulent, mistyped, or malicious registrations while ensuring only verified users can engage with learning content.

Happy Path Steps

Initialize Registration: User completes the sign-up form and submits a valid email address along with their chosen credentials.

Verification Email Dispatched: System generates a secure, time-bound, single-use verification token and sends an email containing a unique activation link.

Link Activation: User opens the email and clicks the verification link within the 24-hour validity window.

Token Validation: System checks the token's authenticity, expiration status, and single-use flag against the stored record.

Account Activation: Upon successful validation, the system marks the account as "Verified," updates the database record, and grants full platform access.

Acceptance Criteria

Verification link must remain valid for exactly 24 hours from the time of dispatch; it is automatically invalidated thereafter.

Users must be blocked from logging in or accessing core features until their email address is verified.

A "Resend Verification" option must always be available so users can request a fresh link if the original is lost, expired, or undelivered.

Exception Handling

E-01: Verification Link Expired. Trigger: The user clicks the verification link after its 24-hour validity period has expired. Resolution: The system invalidates the expired token, displays an expiration message, and allows the user to generate and send a new verification email.

E-02: Invalid or Tampered Verification Token. Trigger: The verification token is modified, corrupted, or does not exist. Resolution: The request is rejected, the event is logged for security auditing, and the user is prompted to request a new verification email.

E-03: Email Delivery Failure. Trigger: The verification email cannot be delivered due to SMTP failure or an invalid email address. Resolution: The system automatically retries delivery and allows the user to resend the email or update the address if all retries fail.

E-04: Multiple Verification Attempts. Trigger: The verification link is clicked more than once after the account has already been activated. Resolution: The system detects the account is already verified and redirects the user to the Login page without altering account status.

E-05: Account Already Verified. Trigger: A verification request is received for an account that is already active. Resolution: The system ignores the duplicate request and informs the user that the account is already verified.

E-06: Email Relay or Mail Service Blocked. Trigger: The recipient's mail provider blocks or bounces the verification email. Resolution: The system logs the delivery failure, notifies the user, and offers the option to update the email address or resend the verification message.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

User clicks a valid verification link

Account is verified and the user is redirected to Login/Dashboard.

TC-002

User clicks an expired verification link

System displays an expiration message and prompts a new verification email.

TC-003

User clicks the verification link twice

System reports the account is already verified without changing state.

TC-004

User requests a resend of the verification email

A new verification email is sent and the previous token is invalidated.

TC-005

User attempts to log in before verification

Login is blocked and a verification prompt is displayed.

TC-006

Tampered verification token is submitted

Verification fails securely without exposing internal system details.

TC-007

Verification completed after a network interruption

Account activates successfully once connectivity is restored and the retry succeeds.



ONB-US-03: Forgot Password & Reset STATUS: In Development    PRIORITY: High    ACTOR: Learner

Intent: To allow a learner to securely regain access to their account when their password is forgotten, without exposing sensitive account information or compromising platform security.

Happy Path Steps

Initiate Reset: User selects "Forgot Password" from the login screen.

Identity Submission: User enters the email address associated with their account.

Reset Link Delivery: System generates a single-use, time-bound reset token and emails a secure reset link.

Password Update: User clicks the link and sets a new password that satisfies the platform's password policy.

Re-authentication: User logs in successfully using the newly created password.

Acceptance Criteria

The reset token must be single-use and automatically invalidated once consumed or expired.

The new password must be validated against the platform's strong password policy before being accepted.

All existing active sessions must be revoked once the password reset is completed, forcing re-authentication everywhere.

Exception Handling

E-01: Password Reset Link Expired. Trigger: The user opens the reset link after it has expired. Resolution: The system invalidates the link and prompts the user to request a new password reset email.

E-02: Weak Password. Trigger: The entered password does not satisfy the password policy (length, complexity, etc.). Resolution: The password update is rejected and the user is shown the specific policy requirements that were not met.

E-03: Previously Used Password. Trigger: The user attempts to reuse a recent password. Resolution: The system rejects the password and asks the user to choose a different one.

E-04: Invalid or Unregistered Email. Trigger: An email not associated with any account is entered. Resolution: A generic confirmation message is displayed without revealing whether the account exists, preventing account enumeration.

E-05: Excessive Reset Requests. Trigger: Multiple reset requests are submitted in a short period. Resolution: The system rate-limits further requests and informs the user to try again later.

E-06: Server Failure. Trigger: A backend error occurs while processing the request. Resolution: The system retries automatically, preserves the original request, and notifies the user if another attempt is required.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

Registered email entered

Password reset email is sent.

TC-002

Unregistered email entered

Generic confirmation shown without revealing account existence.

TC-003

Expired reset link opened

User is prompted to request a new reset link.

TC-004

Weak password entered

Password policy validation error is displayed.

TC-005

Successful password reset

User can log in only with the new password; old sessions are revoked.

TC-006

Reuse of previous password attempted

System rejects the reused password.

TC-007

Invalid reset token submitted

Password reset is denied securely without exposing system details.



ONB-US-04: Profile Management STATUS: In Development    PRIORITY: High    ACTOR: Learner

Intent: To give learners full control over their personal profile and preferences, ensuring changes are validated, synchronized across devices, and traceable for accountability.

Happy Path Steps

Access Profile: User navigates to the Profile section of the platform.

Edit Information: User updates fields such as display name, photo, or preferred language.

Save Changes: User submits the updated information, which passes validation checks.

Cross-Device Sync: System propagates the updated profile data to all of the user's connected devices and logs the change for audit purposes.

Acceptance Criteria

Profile changes must synchronize consistently across all devices the user is signed into.

All mandatory fields must be validated before a save is accepted.

Every profile change must be recorded in an audit log for traceability.

Exception Handling

E-01: Invalid Profile Information. Trigger: The user enters invalid or incomplete mandatory information. Resolution: Invalid fields are highlighted inline, and saving is blocked until all fields are corrected.

E-02: Unsupported Profile Image. Trigger: The uploaded image format or resolution is not supported. Resolution: The upload is rejected and the user is prompted to upload a supported image type.

E-03: Network Connection Lost. Trigger: Internet connectivity is lost while changes are being saved. Resolution: Changes are cached locally on the device and synchronized automatically once connectivity is restored.

E-04: Concurrent Profile Updates. Trigger: The profile is edited simultaneously from two different devices. Resolution: The conflict is detected and the latest valid update is preserved as the source of truth.

E-05: Storage Limit Exceeded. Trigger: The uploaded image exceeds the user's allowed storage limit. Resolution: The upload is cancelled and the user is asked to upload a smaller file.

E-06: Session Expired. Trigger: The user's session expires before the save operation completes. Resolution: The user is prompted to sign in again, and any unsaved data is restored where possible.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

Update display name

Profile updates successfully.

TC-002

Upload a valid profile photo

Image is saved and displayed correctly.

TC-003

Upload an unsupported image format

Validation error is displayed.

TC-004

Update preferred language

Interface reflects the newly selected language.

TC-005

Save profile with missing mandatory fields

Save is blocked until all required fields are valid.

TC-006

Concurrent profile edits from two devices

The latest valid update is persisted.



ONB-US-05: Session & Device Management STATUS: In Development    PRIORITY: High    ACTOR: Learner

Intent: To give learners visibility and control over which devices are logged into their account, enabling them to detect suspicious activity and remotely terminate sessions for security.

Happy Path Steps

Access Security Settings: User navigates to the Security section of account settings.

View Active Devices: System displays a list of all devices with active sessions, including device type, location, and last active time.

Terminate Session: User selects a specific device and logs it out remotely.

Acceptance Criteria

All currently active devices/sessions must be visible to the user in real time.

Remote logout must immediately and reliably terminate the targeted session.

Exception Handling

E-01: Unrecognized Device Login. Trigger: A login occurs from a new, unrecognized device or location. Resolution: The user receives a security alert and is asked to verify or deny the activity.

E-02: Expired Authentication Token. Trigger: The session token expires while the user is managing devices. Resolution: The user is redirected to re-authenticate before continuing.

E-03: Device Synchronization Failure. Trigger: The active device list fails to synchronize with the backend. Resolution: The system retries synchronization and displays the last known device list in the interim.

E-04: Forced Logout. Trigger: An administrator terminates a user's session. Resolution: The user is logged out immediately and informed that the session was ended administratively.

E-05: Offline Device. Trigger: The selected device is offline at the moment logout is requested. Resolution: The logout request is queued and executed automatically once the device reconnects.

E-06: Excessive Active Sessions. Trigger: The maximum number of concurrent sessions is exceeded. Resolution: The oldest session is terminated automatically, or the user is prompted to remove an existing session manually.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

View active sessions

All active devices are displayed.

TC-002

Log out from one device

Only the selected session is terminated.

TC-003

Log out from all devices

All sessions are invalidated simultaneously.

TC-004

Session token expires

User is redirected to the login page.

TC-005

Login occurs from an unknown device

A security notification is generated.

TC-006

Multiple simultaneous logins occur

Sessions are managed and displayed correctly.



ONB-US-06: Privacy & Consent STATUS: In Development    PRIORITY: High    ACTOR: Learner

Intent: To ensure learners can transparently view, manage, and update their privacy and consent preferences in compliance with data protection regulations, while maintaining a full auditable history of changes.

Happy Path Steps

Access Privacy Settings: User navigates to the Privacy section of account settings.

Update Consent Preferences: User modifies consent options, such as marketing communications or data sharing.

Save Preferences: System stores the updated consent version and timestamps the change for audit purposes.

Acceptance Criteria

Every consent decision must be stored with its corresponding policy version.

All consent changes must be fully auditable, with a viewable history available to the user.

Exception Handling

E-01: Mandatory Consent Withdrawn. Trigger: The user attempts to withdraw a legally required consent. Resolution: The system blocks the withdrawal for mandatory items and explains why the consent cannot be revoked while keeping the account active.

E-02: Save Failed. Trigger: A backend error occurs while saving consent preferences. Resolution: The system retries the save and notifies the user if the change could not be persisted.

E-03: Version Mismatch. Trigger: The user's consent is tied to an outdated policy version. Resolution: The user is prompted to review and reaccept the current policy version before proceeding.

E-04: Offline. Trigger: The device loses connectivity while updating consent. Resolution: The change is cached locally and submitted automatically once connectivity is restored.

E-05: Legal Update Pending. Trigger: A new legal/policy update is in the process of being applied to the platform. Resolution: The user is informed that an update is pending and asked to review it once it becomes available.

E-06: Data Request Pending. Trigger: The user has an active data access or deletion request in progress. Resolution: Consent changes are still permitted, but the system notes that the pending data request will be processed independently.

ONB-US-07: Account Deletion US-001: Email Verification & Account Activation

STATUS: In Development    PRIORITY: High    ACTOR: New Learner

Intent: To confirm the authenticity of a new learner's email address before granting full account access, protecting the platform from fraudulent, mistyped, or malicious registrations while ensuring only verified users can engage with learning content.

Happy Path Steps

Initialize Registration: User completes the sign-up form and submits a valid email address along with their chosen credentials.

Verification Email Dispatched: System generates a secure, time-bound, single-use verification token and sends an email containing a unique activation link.

Link Activation: User opens the email and clicks the verification link within the 24-hour validity window.

Token Validation: System checks the token's authenticity, expiration status, and single-use flag against the stored record.

Account Activation: Upon successful validation, the system marks the account as "Verified," updates the database record, and grants full platform access.

Acceptance Criteria

Verification link must remain valid for exactly 24 hours from the time of dispatch; it is automatically invalidated thereafter.

Users must be blocked from logging in or accessing core features until their email address is verified.

A "Resend Verification" option must always be available so users can request a fresh link if the original is lost, expired, or undelivered.

Exception Handling

E-01: Verification Link Expired. Trigger: The user clicks the verification link after its 24-hour validity period has expired. Resolution: The system invalidates the expired token, displays an expiration message, and allows the user to generate and send a new verification email.

E-02: Invalid or Tampered Verification Token. Trigger: The verification token is modified, corrupted, or does not exist. Resolution: The request is rejected, the event is logged for security auditing, and the user is prompted to request a new verification email.

E-03: Email Delivery Failure. Trigger: The verification email cannot be delivered due to SMTP failure or an invalid email address. Resolution: The system automatically retries delivery and allows the user to resend the email or update the address if all retries fail.

E-04: Multiple Verification Attempts. Trigger: The verification link is clicked more than once after the account has already been activated. Resolution: The system detects the account is already verified and redirects the user to the Login page without altering account status.

E-05: Account Already Verified. Trigger: A verification request is received for an account that is already active. Resolution: The system ignores the duplicate request and informs the user that the account is already verified.

E-06: Email Relay or Mail Service Blocked. Trigger: The recipient's mail provider blocks or bounces the verification email. Resolution: The system logs the delivery failure, notifies the user, and offers the option to update the email address or resend the verification message.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

User clicks a valid verification link

Account is verified and the user is redirected to Login/Dashboard.

TC-002

User clicks an expired verification link

System displays an expiration message and prompts a new verification email.

TC-003

User clicks the verification link twice

System reports the account is already verified without changing state.

TC-004

User requests a resend of the verification email

A new verification email is sent and the previous token is invalidated.

TC-005

User attempts to log in before verification

Login is blocked and a verification prompt is displayed.

TC-006

Tampered verification token is submitted

Verification fails securely without exposing internal system details.

TC-007

Verification completed after a network interruption

Account activates successfully once connectivity is restored and the retry succeeds.



US-002: Forgot Password & Reset

STATUS: In Development    PRIORITY: High    ACTOR: Learner

Intent: To allow a learner to securely regain access to their account when their password is forgotten, without exposing sensitive account information or compromising platform security.

Happy Path Steps

Initiate Reset: User selects "Forgot Password" from the login screen.

Identity Submission: User enters the email address associated with their account.

Reset Link Delivery: System generates a single-use, time-bound reset token and emails a secure reset link.

Password Update: User clicks the link and sets a new password that satisfies the platform's password policy.

Re-authentication: User logs in successfully using the newly created password.

Acceptance Criteria

The reset token must be single-use and automatically invalidated once consumed or expired.

The new password must be validated against the platform's strong password policy before being accepted.

All existing active sessions must be revoked once the password reset is completed, forcing re-authentication everywhere.

Exception Handling

E-01: Password Reset Link Expired. Trigger: The user opens the reset link after it has expired. Resolution: The system invalidates the link and prompts the user to request a new password reset email.

E-02: Weak Password. Trigger: The entered password does not satisfy the password policy (length, complexity, etc.). Resolution: The password update is rejected and the user is shown the specific policy requirements that were not met.

E-03: Previously Used Password. Trigger: The user attempts to reuse a recent password. Resolution: The system rejects the password and asks the user to choose a different one.

E-04: Invalid or Unregistered Email. Trigger: An email not associated with any account is entered. Resolution: A generic confirmation message is displayed without revealing whether the account exists, preventing account enumeration.

E-05: Excessive Reset Requests. Trigger: Multiple reset requests are submitted in a short period. Resolution: The system rate-limits further requests and informs the user to try again later.

E-06: Server Failure. Trigger: A backend error occurs while processing the request. Resolution: The system retries automatically, preserves the original request, and notifies the user if another attempt is required.

TC-002

Unregistered email entered

TC-004

Weak password entered

Password policy validation error is displayed.

TC-005

Successful password reset

User can log in only with the new password; old sessions are revoked.

TC-006

Reuse of previous password attempted

System rejects the reused password.

TC-007

Invalid reset token submitted

Password reset is denied securely without exposing system details.



US-003: Profile Management

STATUS: In Development    PRIORITY: High    ACTOR: Learner

Intent: To give learners full control over their personal profile and preferences, ensuring changes are validated, synchronized across devices, and traceable for accountability.

Happy Path Steps

Access Profile: User navigates to the Profile section of the platform.

Edit Information: User updates fields such as display name, photo, or preferred language.

Save Changes: User submits the updated information, which passes validation checks.

Cross-Device Sync: System propagates the updated profile data to all of the user's connected devices and logs the change for audit purposes.

Acceptance Criteria

Profile changes must synchronize consistently across all devices the user is signed into.

All mandatory fields must be validated before a save is accepted.

Every profile change must be recorded in an audit log for traceability.

Exception Handling

E-01: Invalid Profile Information. Trigger: The user enters invalid or incomplete mandatory information. Resolution: Invalid fields are highlighted inline, and saving is blocked until all fields are corrected.

E-02: Unsupported Profile Image. Trigger: The uploaded image format or resolution is not supported. Resolution: The upload is rejected and the user is prompted to upload a supported image type.

E-03: Network Connection Lost. Trigger: Internet connectivity is lost while changes are being saved. Resolution: Changes are cached locally on the device and synchronized automatically once connectivity is restored.

E-04: Concurrent Profile Updates. Trigger: The profile is edited simultaneously from two different devices. Resolution: The conflict is detected and the latest valid update is preserved as the source of truth.

E-05: Storage Limit Exceeded. Trigger: The uploaded image exceeds the user's allowed storage limit. Resolution: The upload is cancelled and the user is asked to upload a smaller file.

E-06: Session Expired. Trigger: The user's session expires before the save operation completes. Resolution: The user is prompted to sign in again, and any unsaved data is restored where possible.

Acceptance Criteria

All currently active devices/sessions must be visible to the user in real time.

Remote logout must immediately and reliably terminate the targeted session.

Exception Handling

E-02: Expired Authentication Token. Trigger: The session token expires while the user is managing devices. Resolution: The user is redirected to re-authenticate before continuing.

E-03: Device Synchronization Failure. Trigger: The active device list fails to synchronize with the backend. Resolution: The system retries synchronization and displays the last known device list in the interim.

E-04: Forced Logout. Trigger: An administrator terminates a user's session. Resolution: The user is logged out immediately and informed that the session was ended administratively.

E-05: Offline Device. Trigger: The selected device is offline at the moment logout is requested. Resolution: The logout request is queued and executed automatically once the device reconnects.

E-06: Excessive Active Sessions. Trigger: The maximum number of concurrent sessions is exceeded. Resolution: The oldest session is terminated automatically, or the user is prompted to remove an existing session manually.

US-005: Account Deletion

STATUS: In Development    PRIORITY: High    ACTOR: Learner

Intent: To allow learners to permanently and securely delete their account and associated data in a manner that is fully compliant with GDPR and other data protection regulations, while safeguarding against accidental or malicious deletion requests.

Happy Path Steps

Initiate Deletion: User navigates to account settings and selects "Delete Account."

Request Confirmation: System prompts the user to confirm the deletion request.

Identity Reverification: User re-enters their password (or completes an equivalent identity check) to confirm intent.

Grace Period: System schedules the account for deletion after a defined grace period, during which the user may cancel.

Permanent Deletion: Once the grace period elapses, the system permanently deletes the account and all associated data, logging the action for compliance.

Acceptance Criteria

Identity must be reverified before any deletion request is accepted.

Every deletion action must be logged for compliance and audit purposes.

The deletion process must fully comply with GDPR (or equivalent) data protection requirements, including complete data erasure.

Exception Handling

E-01: Incorrect Password. Trigger: Identity verification fails during the deletion request. Resolution: The deletion request is rejected until identity is successfully verified.

E-02: Active Subscription. Trigger: The account has an active paid subscription. Resolution: The user is asked to cancel the subscription before the deletion can proceed.

E-03: Pending Financial Transaction. Trigger: Outstanding payments or refunds exist on the account. Resolution: Deletion is postponed until all pending transactions are resolved.

E-04: Administrative or Legal Hold. Trigger: The account is under investigation or subject to legal data retention requirements. Resolution: Deletion is suspended until the hold is officially removed.

E-05: Recovery During Grace Period. Trigger: The user requests account restoration before the grace period expires. Resolution: The deletion request is cancelled and the account, along with its data, is fully restored.

E-06: Backend Deletion Failure. Trigger: A system error occurs during the permanent deletion process. Resolution: The system retries the deletion, logs the failure for investigation, and notifies the user once the deletion is successfully completed.

Validation Test Cases

 

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

Delete account with confirmation

Account is scheduled for deletion / deleted successfully.

TC-002

Cancel deletion request

Account remains active.

TC-003

Incorrect password entered during confirmation

Deletion is denied.

TC-004

Attempt login after deletion

Access is blocked entirely.

TC-005

Recover account within the grace period

Account is fully restored.

TC-006

Deletion occurs after the grace period

Data is permanently removed in accordance with policy.

ONB-US-09: Apple SSO Authentication & Privacy Flow

STATUS: In Development PRIORITY: High ACTOR: New Learner

Intent: To securely register for the platform using "Sign in with Apple," specifically utilizing Apple's "Hide My Email" privacy functionality.

Happy Path Steps

Initiation: User taps "Continue with Apple" on the onboarding screen.

OS Authentication: iOS prompts the user for FaceID/TouchID and asks if they wish to share or hide their email address.

Selection: User selects "Hide My Email."

Token Exchange: Apple generates a unique proxy email and passes the authentication token to the Speeky-AI backend.

Account Creation: Speeky-AI creates the user profile linked to the proxy email.

Acceptance Criteria

The system must correctly route all platform emails (e.g., Welcome Email, Password Resets) through Apple's private relay service.

The user's progress and profile must persist regardless of whether they chose to hide or share their email.

Exception Handling

E-01: Apple Relay Email Bounce. The system attempts to send a notification, but the user has deactivated the Apple proxy email via their iCloud settings. RESOLUTION: System logs a soft bounce, disables further marketing emails to that address, and prompts the user to update their email upon next login.

E-02: Revoked App Access. User revokes Speeky-AI access via their iOS settings and tries to log in again. RESOLUTION: The backend detects an invalid token, forces a re-authentication flow, and seamlessly reconnects them to their existing profile using their Apple ID hash.

E-03: Switching Platforms (iOS to Android). An Apple SSO user attempts to log into the Android app. RESOLUTION: App implements a web-based Apple OAuth fallback for non-iOS devices, allowing cross-platform access.

Baseline Assessment & Confidence Scoring

BAS-US-01: Baseline Assessment Results Summary View

STATUS: Not Started (Gap)   PRIORITY: High   ACTOR: New Learner

Intent: To view a clear, encouraging summary of their initial assessment results (learning level and confidence score breakdown) immediately after completing the baseline test, so they understand where they are starting from.

Happy Path Steps

Completion: User finishes the final question of the Initial Communication Assessment (US-002).

Processing: System displays a brief "Analyzing your responses..." loading state.

Reveal: System presents a results screen showing the assigned Learning Level, initial Confidence Score, and a one-line breakdown across Fluency, Vocabulary, Pronunciation, and Confidence.

Framing: System displays an encouraging message positioning the score as a starting point, not a grade.

Transition: User taps "Start Learning" to proceed to their personalized dashboard and learning path.

Acceptance Criteria

Results screen must appear within 10 seconds of assessment completion.

Must display all four scored metrics plus the aggregated top-line Confidence Score.

Language must frame results positively regardless of score (no "failing" language).

Exception Handling

E-01: Processing Delay. AI scoring takes longer than 10 seconds. RESOLUTION: Show an animated progress indicator with reassuring copy ("Almost done crunching your results") rather than a blank screen.

E-02: Scoring Engine Failure. Backend fails to return a score after assessment completion. RESOLUTION: Save the raw responses, notify the user their results are "still processing," and retry scoring in the background, notifying the user when ready.

E-03: User Force-Closes App Before Reveal. User exits immediately after finishing the last question, before seeing results. RESOLUTION: Persist the computed results so they display automatically the next time the app opens.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

Standard voice assessment completion

Results screen renders all 4 metrics plus Confidence Score within 10 seconds.

TC-002

Scoring takes >10 seconds

Progress indicator with reassuring copy displays instead of a blank screen.

TC-003

Scoring engine returns an error

User sees a "still processing" state; results appear once retry succeeds.

TC-004

App force-closed before reveal screen

On reopen, the previously computed results display automatically.





BAS-US-02: Skip Assessment & Feature-Access Gating

STATUS: Not Started (Gap)   PRIORITY: High   ACTOR: New Learner / System

Intent: To define what happens when a new learner attempts to bypass or skip the mandatory baseline assessment, ensuring the app maintains a valid confidence-score foundation for every learner before unlocking coaching features.

Happy Path Steps

Attempt: New learner taps "Skip" or navigates away from the assessment intro screen.

Warning: System displays a modal explaining that all coaching features require a baseline score to personalize practice.

Choice: User confirms the skip or returns to start the assessment.

Provisional State: If the user confirms skip, system assigns a default "Unassessed" learning level and locks personalized modules.

Reminder: System resurfaces a persistent, non-blocking prompt to complete the assessment on subsequent logins.

Acceptance Criteria

Must not allow access to AI Conversation Practice, Interview Coach, or Scenario-Based Learning while status is "Unassessed."

Must allow access to app settings and account management while unassessed.

Skip prompt must be shown only once per session, not repeatedly interrupting navigation.

Exception Handling

E-01: Repeated Skipping. User skips the assessment on 3+ consecutive logins. RESOLUTION: Escalate messaging to explain specific feature limitations being missed, without blocking basic account access.

E-02: Partial Then Skip. User starts the assessment, abandons it, then explicitly skips instead of resuming. RESOLUTION: Discard the partial data and set status to "Unassessed" rather than leaving it "In Progress" indefinitely.

E-03: Enterprise-Assigned Learner. A learner added via Enterprise Admin bulk import attempts to skip. RESOLUTION: Honor the org-level policy flag; if the organization requires a mandatory assessment, disable the skip option entirely for that cohort.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

User taps Skip on intro screen

Warning modal appears explaining feature-locking consequences.

TC-002

User confirms skip

Learning level set to "Unassessed"; personalized modules locked; settings remain accessible.

TC-003

Unassessed user tries to open Interview Coach

Access is blocked with a prompt to complete the baseline assessment.

TC-004

Org policy disables skipping

Skip button is hidden/disabled for learners under that policy.





BAS-US-03: Assessment Integrity & Anti-Gaming Safeguards

STATUS: Not Started (Gap)   PRIORITY: Medium   ACTOR: System

Intent: To detect and prevent learners from artificially inflating their baseline or recalculated Confidence Score through pre-recorded audio, text-to-speech playback, or copy-pasted text answers.

Happy Path Steps

Capture: System records the audio or text response during an assessment or scoring session.

Integrity Check: System runs signal analysis (e.g., waveform consistency, clipboard-paste detection on text fields) alongside scoring.

Pass: If no anomalies are detected, scoring proceeds normally.

Flag: If an anomaly is detected, the system marks the response for review rather than scoring it as genuine.

Resolution: System either requests a live re-response or excludes the flagged data point from the Confidence Score calculation.

Acceptance Criteria

System must distinguish synthetic/TTS audio signatures from natural human speech against a documented confidence threshold.

Pasted text answers (via clipboard) must be flagged and excluded from Fluency and Vocabulary scoring.

Flagged sessions must never silently boost the Confidence Score.

Exception Handling

E-01: False Positive on Accented Speech. Legitimate heavy-accent audio is misflagged as synthetic. RESOLUTION: Route to a secondary verification check before excluding; never penalize the user's score for a flagged-but-unconfirmed case.

E-02: Repeated Gaming Attempts. Same user triggers the anti-gaming flag across 3+ sessions. RESOLUTION: Temporarily restrict that user's sessions from contributing to the Confidence Score and surface an account review notice.

E-03: Legitimate Text Paste (Accessibility Tool). User pastes text generated by an approved assistive dictation tool. RESOLUTION: Allow an accessibility opt-in flag on the account that exempts paste detection for that user.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

Submit known TTS-generated audio

System flags the response and excludes it from scoring.

TC-002

Paste text into a free-response field

Response is flagged and excluded from Fluency/Vocabulary scoring.

TC-003

Heavy-accent genuine speech submitted

Secondary verification runs; score is not penalized while unconfirmed.

TC-004

Accessibility opt-in enabled, then text pasted

Paste is not flagged due to the accessibility exemption.







BAS-US-04: On-Demand Re-Assessment Request

STATUS: Not Started (Gap)   PRIORITY: Medium   ACTOR: Learner

Intent: To allow a motivated learner to voluntarily request an early re-assessment before their scheduled 30-day cycle, so they can validate progress on their own timeline.

Happy Path Steps

Request: Learner navigates to their profile/progress area and taps "Retake Baseline Assessment."

Eligibility Check: System checks days elapsed since the last baseline or re-assessment.

Confirmation: If eligible, system confirms and starts the assessment using a fresh passage/question set.

Update: Completed results overwrite the current baseline and are appended to historical trend data, same as the scheduled flow.

Acceptance Criteria

Must clearly state the number of days remaining if the user is not yet eligible for a full re-assessment.

Must allow no more than one voluntary early re-assessment per 30-day cycle to preserve trend data integrity.

Must use the same passage-rotation logic as the scheduled 30-day re-assessment (never repeat the immediately prior passage).

Exception Handling

E-01: Too-Frequent Requests. User requests a second early retake within the same cycle. RESOLUTION: Block the request and display the days remaining until the next eligible window.

E-02: Request During Active Session. User requests a retake while mid-way through an unrelated practice session. RESOLUTION: Queue the retake to begin after the current session ends rather than interrupting it.

E-03: Enterprise Policy Restriction. Learner's organization has disabled early retakes to standardize reporting cadence. RESOLUTION: Hide or disable the "Retake" option entirely for learners under that policy.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

Eligible user requests early retake

Assessment starts immediately with a fresh passage set.

TC-002

Ineligible user requests retake

System displays days remaining and blocks the request.

TC-003

Retake requested mid-session

Retake is queued and begins after the active session ends.

TC-004

Org has disabled early retakes

Retake option is hidden for that learner.



BAS-US-05: Confidence Score Stagnation Detection

STATUS: Not Started (Gap)   PRIORITY: Medium   ACTOR: System

Intent: To detect when a learner's Confidence Score has plateaued over multiple assessment cycles and proactively surface a coaching intervention, rather than only reacting to score regressions.

Happy Path Steps

Trigger: System runs a trend analysis after each periodic re-assessment (BAS-US-12) completes.

Detection: System compares the last 3 consecutive baseline cycles and identifies a change below a defined minimal threshold.

Flag: System classifies the learner as "Plateaued" internally.

Intervention: Dashboard surfaces a proactive nudge suggesting a different practice mode or focus area (e.g., "Try Scenario-Based Learning to break through your plateau").

Reset: The flag clears automatically once the learner's score shows meaningful movement in either direction.

Acceptance Criteria

Stagnation must only be evaluated after a minimum of 3 completed re-assessment cycles exist for the learner.

The nudge must recommend a concrete, specific action, not a generic "keep practicing" message.

Must not trigger alongside the Score Regression flag (E-02 in BAS-US-12) within the same cycle.

Exception Handling

E-01: New Learner Insufficient History. Learner has fewer than 3 re-assessment cycles. RESOLUTION: Suppress stagnation detection entirely until enough historical data points exist.

E-02: Plateau at a High Score Ceiling. Learner's score has plateaued near the top of the scale (e.g., 95+/100). RESOLUTION: Reframe messaging to celebrate mastery rather than suggesting a "fix," offering advanced/expert content instead.

E-03: Inactive Learner. Learner has stopped practicing altogether rather than plateauing while active. RESOLUTION: Route to re-engagement messaging instead of stagnation coaching, since the flat score reflects inactivity, not a skill ceiling.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

3 consecutive cycles with <2% change

Learner is flagged "Plateaued" and a specific nudge is surfaced.

TC-002

Fewer than 3 cycles completed

Stagnation detection is suppressed.

TC-003

Plateau at 96/100 score

Mastery-celebration messaging shown instead of a generic "fix" prompt.

TC-004

Flat score due to 60 days of inactivity

Re-engagement messaging shown instead of stagnation coaching.



BAS-US-06: Confidence Score Explainability Breakdown

STATUS: Not Started (Gap)   PRIORITY: Medium   ACTOR: Learner

Intent: To let a learner tap into their Confidence Score at any time and see a clear, plain-language explanation of how it was calculated, building trust in the "confidence over grammar" scoring philosophy.

Happy Path Steps

Access: Learner taps an info icon or "Why this score?" link next to their Confidence Score widget.

Breakdown Display: System displays the underlying metric contributions (Fluency, Vocabulary, Pronunciation) and their relative weighting.

Plain-Language Summary: System generates a short natural-language explanation of the current score, referencing the recent sessions that most influenced it.

History Link: User can tap through to view the historical trend line feeding the current calculation.

Acceptance Criteria

Breakdown must never expose raw internal formula weights as a literal equation; it must be translated into learner-friendly language.

Must always reflect the exact data used in the most recent recalculation (no stale caching beyond one session).

Must be accessible from both the main dashboard widget and the results summary screen (GAP-01).

Exception Handling

E-01: Text-Only User Requests Breakdown. User's recent sessions were entirely text-mode, so Pronunciation is excluded. RESOLUTION: Explicitly state "Pronunciation not included — no voice sessions this period" rather than showing a blank or zero value.

E-02: Breakdown Requested Immediately Post-Signup. New learner has zero session history. RESOLUTION: Display an empty state directing them to complete the Initial Communication Assessment first.

E-03: Conflicting Data During Recalculation. User requests the breakdown while a background score update (per BAS-US-10) is mid-write. RESOLUTION: Show the last stable, fully-committed score rather than a partially updated value.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

Tap "Why this score?" with full session history

Plain-language breakdown displays all 3 metric contributions.

TC-002

Request breakdown as a text-only user

Pronunciation is explicitly labeled as excluded rather than blank.

TC-003

Request breakdown with zero sessions

Empty state directs the user to complete the Initial Assessment.

TC-004

Request breakdown mid-recalculation

Last stable committed score is shown, not a partial value.



BAS-US-07: Admin Configuration of Confidence Scoring Weights

STATUS: Not Started (Gap)   PRIORITY: Low   ACTOR: Platform Admin / Ops

Intent: To allow an authorized internal admin to adjust the relative weighting of Fluency, Vocabulary, and Pronunciation in the Confidence Score formula without a code deployment, enabling data-driven tuning of the "confidence over grammar" philosophy.

Happy Path Steps

Access: Admin navigates to the internal Scoring Configuration panel.

Adjustment: Admin modifies the weight values for each metric, with the total constrained to 100%.

Preview: System shows the simulated impact on a sample of anonymized learner scores before applying.

Publish: Admin confirms and publishes the new weighting, versioned with a timestamp and author.

Rollout: New weighting applies to all subsequent score recalculations going forward; historical scores remain unchanged.

Acceptance Criteria

Weight changes must never retroactively alter previously calculated and stored historical scores.

System must require the three weights to sum to 100% before allowing publish.

Every weight change must be logged with admin identity, timestamp, and previous vs. new values for audit purposes.

Exception Handling

E-01: Invalid Weight Total. Admin submits weights that sum to more or less than 100%. RESOLUTION: Block publish and display the current total with an inline validation error.

E-02: Concurrent Admin Edits. Two admins attempt to publish conflicting weight changes simultaneously. RESOLUTION: Use last-confirmed-write-wins with a warning shown to the second admin, and preserve the full change log so the earlier change is never silently lost.

E-03: Emergency Rollback Needed. A new weighting causes unexpected score volatility in production. RESOLUTION: Provide a one-click "Revert to previous version" action from the audit log.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

Admin sets weights summing to 100%

Preview renders; publish succeeds and is timestamped/logged.

TC-002

Admin sets weights summing to 92%

Publish is blocked with an inline validation error.

TC-003

Two admins publish conflicting changes

Last confirmed write applies; both changes appear in the audit log.

TC-004

Admin triggers rollback after volatility

Previous weighting version is restored with one click.



BAS-US-08: Foreign-Script / Transliterated Text Detection During Assessment

STATUS: Not Started (Gap)   PRIORITY: Low   ACTOR: New Learner / System

Intent: To correctly detect and handle non-English script or transliterated text entered during the text-mode Initial Communication Assessment, complementing the existing audio-based non-English detection.

Happy Path Steps

Input: User types a response using a non-Latin script (e.g., Devanagari, Arabic) or a romanized transliteration of their native language.

Detection: System's language-detection layer flags the input as non-English.

Redirect: AI responds with the same English-only guidance used for spoken non-English input, adapted for text.

Retry: User re-submits a response in English, and scoring proceeds normally.

Acceptance Criteria

Must apply the same non-English handling used in audio mode (E-05 of US-002) consistently to text-mode input.

Must correctly distinguish genuine non-English script from English words containing accented characters or proper nouns (e.g., "café," "José").

Must not count a flagged non-English attempt as a scored response.

Exception Handling

E-01: Mixed-Language Response. User writes a sentence that is mostly English with a few native-language words inserted. RESOLUTION: Score the response normally but flag the non-English words as unscored vocabulary rather than rejecting the whole answer.

E-02: Transliterated Native Language. User types their native language phonetically in Latin script (e.g., Urdu written in Roman letters). RESOLUTION: Detect via language-model confidence scoring rather than script-only detection, and apply the standard non-English redirection.

E-03: False Positive on Proper Nouns. Response is valid English but contains a foreign proper noun (e.g., a city or name). RESOLUTION: Do not flag responses solely for isolated proper nouns; require broader non-English content to trigger the redirect.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-001

Response typed entirely in Arabic script

System flags as non-English and redirects with English-only guidance.

TC-002

Mostly-English sentence with 2 native words

Response is scored; native words flagged as unscored vocabulary only.

TC-003

Urdu written phonetically in Latin letters

Language-model detection flags it as non-English despite Latin script.

TC-004

Valid English sentence containing "José"

Response is not flagged; scoring proceeds normally.





BAS-US-09: Initial Communication Assessment

STATUS: In Development PRIORITY: High ACTOR: New Learner

Intent: To complete a 5-minute AI-led evaluation to establish a baseline confidence and learning level.

Happy Path Steps

Initiate Assessment: Right after registration, user starts the assessment.

AI Inquiry: AI asks introductory questions.

User Response: User responds via voice or text.

Evaluation: AI processes input and evaluates fluency, pronunciation, confidence, and vocabulary.

Result Generation: System assigns a learning level and initial confidence score.

Acceptance Criteria

Assessment must be approximately 5 minutes long (low-effort).

AI must return scores across all four defined metrics.

Must process both audio transcription and text inputs.

Exception Handling

E-01: Hardware Permission Denied. OS blocks microphone access. RESOLUTION: Display instructions to enable mic in settings, or offer to switch to text mode.

E-02: Silent Audio Detection. Microphone is active but no decibel input is detected during the recording window. RESOLUTION: AI prompts: "I didn't hear anything. Let's try again, or you can type your answer."

E-03: High Background Noise. High ambient noise interferes with transcription. RESOLUTION: Show warning: "Too much background noise. Move to a quieter area for an accurate score."

E-04: Gibberish/Nonsense Text Input. User types random characters instead of words. RESOLUTION: AI flags input as unscorable and requests a real sentence.

E-05: Non-English Speech Detected. User speaks in a language other than English. RESOLUTION: AI politely states, "I only understand English right now. Let's try answering in English."

E-06: Early Abandonment. User closes app mid-assessment. RESOLUTION: Save session state. Prompt user to resume or restart upon next login.

Validation Test Cases

 Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

 TC-0 01

Complete voice assessment

Generates baseline scores across all 4 metrics.

 TC-0 02

Complete text assessment

Generates scores (pronunciation score is N/A or estimated).

 TC-0 03

Hardware permission blocked

Prompts text-mode fallback or settings redirect.

 TC-0 04

Audio with >70db background noise

Triggers "Background noise" warning UI.

 TC-0 05

App closed during question 2

On reopen, user resumes at question 2.

BAS-US-10: Confidence Score Re-Calculation Engine

STATUS: In Development PRIORITY: High ACTOR: System / Learner

Intent: To automatically measure and update the user's top-line communication confidence metric dynamically after every interaction.

Happy Path Steps

Trigger: Learner completes any standard practice session, mock interview, or scenario.

Data Aggregation: System captures the raw scores for fluency, vocabulary, and pronunciation from that session.

Calculation: The engine calculates a weighted average of the new session data against historical data.

Update: The central Confidence Score updates, and the new score is pushed to the Progress Dashboard.

Acceptance Criteria

The Confidence Score must serve as the single top-line metric shown across the app.

The calculation must reframe progress around confidence rather than strict grammar correctness.

Exception Handling

E-01: Extreme Outlier Score. A user scores 10/100 on a session due to audio failure, compared to their usual 85/100. RESOLUTION: System flags the score as a >50% variance outlier and drops it from the weighted average to prevent artificially tanking the user's confidence score.

E-02: Abandoned Session. User exits a session halfway through. RESOLUTION: The system discards the partial data and does not recalculate the Confidence Score.

E-03: Backend Database Timeout. The scoring engine fails to write the new score to the database within 5 seconds. RESOLUTION: System queues the score update locally and retries the sync in the background.

E-04: Null Pronunciation Score (Text Mode). User completes a text-only AI Conversation session. RESOLUTION: System omits Pronunciation from the calculation formula for that specific session, weighting only Vocabulary and Fluency.

Validation Test Cases

 Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

 TC-0 01

Complete voice session

Confidence score recalculates and updates on the dashboard.

 TC-0 02

Complete text session

Calculation correctly ignores pronunciation and updates score based on text metrics.

 TC-0 03

Extreme audio outlier score

System identifies outlier anomaly and prevents score tanking.

 TC-0 04

Mid-session abandonment

No data is passed to the engine; score remains unchanged.

 TC-0 05

Top-line UI visibility

Updated score reflects instantly on the main home screen widget.

BAS-US-11: Confidence vs. Grammar Feedback Focus

STATUS: In Development PRIORITY: High (Core Philosophy) ACTOR: Learner / System

Intent: To evaluate the user based on successful communication and confidence rather than strict grammatical perfection, aligning with the "Grammarly for Spoken English" philosophy.

Happy Path Steps

Execution: User completes a Scenario-Based Learning session (e.g., Airport).

Analysis: The AI processes the transcript and identifies minor grammatical errors (e.g., "I go to airport yesterday") alongside successful communication of intent.

Feedback Generation: The system highlights the successful intent (e.g., "The customs officer understood your destination") and boosts the Confidence Score.

Grammar De-prioritization: Grammar corrections are placed in a secondary "Minor Polish" section rather than being flagged as critical failures.

Acceptance Criteria

The primary metric displayed must be the Confidence Score, not a grammar accuracy percentage.

The AI must not interrupt an active conversation to correct minor tense errors if the meaning is clear.

Exception Handling

E-01: Unintelligible Grammar. The grammatical structure is so broken that the AI persona cannot understand the intent (e.g., "Airport go I why no").

RESOLUTION: AI breaks from the confidence-first model to prompt: "I didn't quite understand that. Are you trying to say...?"

E-02: Professional Context Violation. The user makes a minor grammar error in a high-stakes Workplace Email scenario. RESOLUTION: The system dynamically tightens the grammar penalty, as written workplace communication demands higher accuracy than casual speech.

E-03: Repeat Grammatical Offender. The user makes the exact same tense error 10 times in a session. RESOLUTION: System logs a specific actionable tip in the feedback summary (e.g., "Review Past Tense Verbs") without tanking the overarching Confidence Score.

Validation Test Cases

 Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

 TC-0 01

Minor grammar error (Casual)

Confidence score remains high; grammar noted as minor polish.

 TC-0 02

Minor grammar error (Email)

Grammar error flagged distinctly due to workplace context.

 TC-0 03

Unintelligible sentence

AI prompts for clarification; penalizes fluency.

 TC-0 04

Repeated tense error

System generates a targeted grammar tip in post-session review.

 TC-0 05

View primary feedback metric

UI prominently displays Confidence Score above all other metrics.

BAS-US-12: Periodic Baseline Re-Assessment

STATUS: In Development PRIORITY: High ACTOR: Learner

Intent: To re-take the baseline communication and accent assessment periodically to officially re-calibrate their learning level and prove long-term progress.

Happy Path Steps

Trigger: After 30 days of active platform usage, the system generates a dashboard prompt: "Time for your Monthly Check-in!"

Execution: User initiates the assessment and reads the provided sample passages aloud.

Analysis: AI evaluates current pronunciation, stress patterns, rhythm, intonation, and clarity.

Comparison: System compares the new baseline against the initial Day 1 profile.

Update: User's overarching learning level is updated, and the Accent Progress Tracker is populated with the new data point.

Acceptance Criteria

The re-assessment must use a different reading passage than the Day 1 test to prevent memorization skewing the score.

The system must save the historical data to populate the month-over-month progress trend lines.

Exception Handling

E-01: User Dismisses Prompt. User clicks "Skip for now" on the re-assessment prompt. RESOLUTION: The prompt minimizes to a subtle dashboard banner and does not interrupt daily learning until the user is ready.

E-02: Score Regression Detected. The new baseline score is significantly lower than the previous month (e.g., due to a cold or bad mic). RESOLUTION:

System flags the anomaly and prompts: "Your score was unusually low today. Do you want to retake the test to ensure accuracy?"

E-03: Partial Completion. User answers the first question but exits the app before finishing the 5-minute assessment. RESOLUTION: Do not update the baseline profile; save the progress and prompt resumption on the next login.

Validation Test Cases

 Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

 TC-0 01

30-day prompt trigger

System successfully displays the re-assessment modal on day 30.

 TC-0 02

Complete re- assessment

New scores overwrite current baseline and append to historical trends.

 TC-0 03

Dismiss assessment

Modal closes and converts into a dismissible dashboard widget.

 TC-0 04

Detect score regression

System catches a >20% drop and offers a voluntary retake.

 TC-0 05

Different passage generation

AI serves passage variant B instead of the Day 1 variant A.

BAS-US-13: Confidence Score Aggregation Engine

STATUS: In Development PRIORITY: High (Core Philosophy) ACTOR: System

Intent: To calculate a centralized, top-line Confidence Score by aggregating the user's fluency, vocabulary, and pronunciation metrics across all sessions, reframing progress positively.

Happy Path Steps

Trigger: User completes any practice session.

Data Extraction: System pulls the raw 0-100 scores for Fluency, Vocabulary, and Pronunciation from the session.

Weighted Calculation: The engine applies a mathematical formula prioritizing Fluency (flow of conversation) over strict grammatical perfection.

Update: The user's global Confidence Score is updated.

Display: The updated score immediately populates the main Progress Dashboard widget.

Acceptance Criteria

The formula must weigh Fluency and Vocabulary usage higher than raw Pronunciation, aligning with the "confidence over grammar" philosophy.

The score must update seamlessly in the background after every completed module.

Exception Handling

E-01: Text-Only Session Scoring. User completes an AI Conversation entirely in text mode. RESOLUTION: The system dynamically recalculates the Confidence Score using only Fluency and Vocabulary, omitting Pronunciation without skewing the average downwards.

E-02: Abandoned Session Zero-Score. User starts a session and closes the app, resulting in a 0/100 score being sent to the database. RESOLUTION:

The aggregation engine filters out sessions flagged as "Incomplete" to prevent artificially tanking the user's Confidence Score.

E-03: Infinite Growth Ceiling. A user practices for 3 years, causing the raw aggregate score to logically exceed 100%. RESOLUTION: The formula utilizes a logarithmic cap, ensuring the score remains a percentage (0-100) or a leveled tier system.

Validation Test Cases

 Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

 TC-0 01

Standard session completion

Global Confidence Score recalculates and updates on the dashboard.

 TC-0 02

Text-mode only completion

Score updates accurately while ignoring pronunciation metrics.

 TC-0 03

Abandoned session filter

0/100 incomplete scores are dropped from the global average.

 TC-0 04

Verify weighting logic

High fluency / low grammar score still yields a positive Confidence boost.

 TC-0 05

Real-time UI refresh

Dashboard widget updates instantly without requiring a manual refresh.

AIC-US-01: Custom / User-Defined Topic Input

STATUS: Proposed PRIORITY: High ACTOR: Learner

Intent: To allow the learner to type or speak a topic of their own choosing when none of the preset menu options (Daily Life, Travel, Technology, Education, Work) match their interest, so practice always feels relevant.

Happy Path Steps

Topic Selection: User taps "Custom Topic" instead of a preset card.

Topic Entry: User types or speaks a free-text topic (e.g., "My favorite video games").

AI Validation: System checks the topic's appropriateness, then confirms with a short preview question.

Initiation: AI opens the conversation with a tailored, on-topic opening question.

Session End: User completes the session and receives feedback tagged under a "Custom" category.

Acceptance Criteria

The system must accept free-text topic input via both typing and voice dictation.

The AI must generate a relevant opening question within 3 seconds.

Custom topics must be logged separately for future "recently practiced" suggestions.

Exception Handling

E-01: Inappropriate Custom Topic. User submits a topic containing explicit, violent, or hateful content. RESOLUTION: System rejects the topic before session start, displays "Please choose a different topic," and does not launch the AI session.

E-02: Topic Too Vague. User enters a single ambiguous word (e.g., "stuff"). RESOLUTION: AI asks a clarifying question before proceeding.

E-03: Topic Matches an Existing Preset. User types "Travel" as free text. RESOLUTION: System silently routes the session into the existing "Travel & Culture" flow.

E-04: Empty Custom Topic Submission. User submits with no text entered. RESOLUTION: The "Start" button stays disabled until at least 3 characters are entered.

E-05: Non-English Topic Entry. User types the topic in a non-English language. RESOLUTION: System detects the language and translates internally, but the conversation itself is conducted in English, and the user is informed of this.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-01

Valid custom topic submitted

AI opens with a relevant question within 3 seconds.

TC-02

Explicit/unsafe topic submitted

Topic is rejected before session start; no AI session is created.

TC-03

Single vague word entered

AI asks a clarifying question instead of guessing the topic.

TC-04

Custom topic duplicates a preset

Session silently uses the existing tuned preset flow.

TC-05

Topic entered in native language

System translates internally and confirms English will be used.



AIC-US-02: Conversation Transcript Review & Replay

STATUS: Proposed PRIORITY: Medium ACTOR: Learner

Intent: To let the learner revisit the full written transcript of a past AI Conversation Practice session, with mistakes highlighted and original audio playable, so they can review and learn afterward.

Happy Path Steps

Navigation: User opens session history and selects a completed session.

Transcript Load: System displays the full turn-by-turn transcript.

Highlighting: Grammar/vocabulary issues are highlighted inline with tooltips.

Audio Playback: For voice turns, the user taps their own turn to play back the original audio.

Exit: User closes the transcript and returns to session history.

Acceptance Criteria

Transcripts must remain available for at least the last 90 days.

Highlighted corrections must match the original post-session scorecard, not be recalculated differently.

Voice recordings must be retrievable and playable inline without leaving the transcript screen.

Exception Handling

E-01: Audio Recording Deleted per Privacy Request. The session's audio was deleted under the Privacy policy. RESOLUTION: Display transcript text only, with a note: "Audio no longer available."

E-02: Corrupted or Incomplete Transcript. An app crash left a partial log. RESOLUTION: Display available turns with a banner: "This session ended unexpectedly; the transcript may be incomplete."

E-03: Very Long Session Transcript. Session reached the maximum length (30+ turns). RESOLUTION: Paginate or lazy-load the transcript to prevent UI lag.

E-04: Transcript Requested Mid-Sync. User opens the transcript while offline, and it hasn't synced from another device yet. RESOLUTION: Show a loading state with a "Sync pending" message instead of an empty screen.

Validation Test Cases

Case ID

Scenario

Expected Result

TC-01
